-- 2021/06/02 : SEQ_CNTNTS_HIST_ID 시퀀스 누락되서 추가
-- 2021/07/02 : 회원Salt값, LoginCnt 컬럼 추가
-- 2021/07/30 : TCO_WH_WIDG_HIST (위젯 백업 테이블), SEQ_WIDG_BAK_SN_SEQ (위젯 백업 시퀀스) , TAP_AM_APPLE_MANAGE (관리자페이지 관리 테이블)
-- 2022/02/21 : 신규위젯 적용
-- 3.0에서 사용하던 SEQ_WIDG_SN, SEQ_WIDG_DATA_SN 최신 위젯에서 활용하게 변경
-- 위젯관리 테이블 : TAP_WM_WIDGET_MANAGE, TAP_WM_WIDGET_DATA, TAP_WM_WIDGET_IMAGE 테이블 추가
-- 위젯이력관리 테이블 : TAP_WM_WIDGET_HIST_MANAGE, TAP_WM_WIDGET_MANAGE_HIST, TAP_WM_WIDGET_DATA_HIST, TAP_WM_WIDGET_IMAGE_HIST 테이블 추가
-- 2022/04/05 : TAP_SM_SYS_MANAGE에 SUB_IMG_ID, LOGO_ID 컬럼 추가
-- 2022/07/26 : svn배포

-- Sequence [QUICK_MANAGE_SN]

MAXVALUE 999999999999999999 
MINVALUE 1 NOCYCLE CACHE 20;

--  Table [TAP_AC_ACS_MANAGE] 

CREATE TABLE TAP_AC_ACS_MANAGE 
(
	ACCES_NO         INT (10) NOT NULL,
	ACCES_TRGET      VARCHAR (256) NOT NULL,
	ACCES_TRGET_PSITN VARCHAR (256) NOT NULL,
	ATHRI_IP         VARCHAR (256) NOT NULL,
	PVTESBL_IP       VARCHAR (256),
	MACADRS          VARCHAR (256),
	IP_SCOPE         VARCHAR (256),
	MBER_ID          VARCHAR (256),
	CREAT_USID       VARCHAR (256) NOT NULL,
	CREAT_IP         VARCHAR (256) NOT NULL,
	CREAT_DT         DATETIME NOT NULL,
	CONFM_AT         CHAR (1) NOT NULL,
	CONFM_ID         VARCHAR (256),
	CONFM_IP         VARCHAR (256),
	CONFM_DT         DATETIME,
	BAND_IP_USE_AT   CHAR (1)
)
;

ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `ACCES_NO` int(10) NOT NULL COMMENT '접근제어번호';
ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `ACCES_TRGET` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '접근제어대상';
ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `ACCES_TRGET_PSITN` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '접근제어대상소속';
ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `ATHRI_IP` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '공인아이피';
ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `PVTESBL_IP` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '사설아이피';
ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `MACADRS` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT 'MAC주소';
ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `IP_SCOPE` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '아이피범위';
ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `BAND_IP_USE_AT` char(1) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '대역 아이피 사용 유무';
ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `MBER_ID` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '회원아이디';
ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `CREAT_USID` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '신청아이디';
ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `CREAT_IP` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '신청아이피';
ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `CREAT_DT` datetime NOT NULL COMMENT '신청일';
ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `CONFM_AT` char(1) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '승인여부';
ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `CONFM_ID` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '승인아이디';
ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `CONFM_IP` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '승인아이피';
ALTER TABLE tap_ac_acs_manage MODIFY COLUMN `CONFM_DT` datetime DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '승인일';



--  Table [TAP_AU_AUTHOR_HIST] 

CREATE TABLE TAP_AU_AUTHOR_HIST 
(
	AUTHOR_MBER_SEQ  INT (10) NOT NULL,
	MBER_ID          VARCHAR (256) NOT NULL,
	AUTHOR_CODE      INT (16),
	SYS_ID           VARCHAR (20),
	HIST_SEQ         INT (10) NOT NULL,
	HIST_GROUP_SEQ   INT (10),
	HIST_USER_ID     VARCHAR (256),
	HIST_USER_NM     VARCHAR (256),
	HIST_USER_IP     VARCHAR (256),
	HIST_DATE        DATETIME,
	HIST_TY          CHAR (1)
)
;

ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_hist COMMENT='사용자 권한 이력 관리';

ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_hist MODIFY COLUMN `AUTHOR_MBER_SEQ` int(10) NOT NULL COMMENT '사용자권한번호';
ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_hist MODIFY COLUMN `MBER_ID` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '사용자 아이디';
ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_hist MODIFY COLUMN `AUTHOR_CODE` int(16) DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '권한코드';
ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_hist MODIFY COLUMN `SYS_ID` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '시스템 아이디';
ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_hist MODIFY COLUMN `HIST_SEQ` int(10) NOT NULL COMMENT '이력번호';
ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_hist MODIFY COLUMN `HIST_GROUP_SEQ` int(10) DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '이력그룹번호';
ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_hist MODIFY COLUMN `HIST_USER_ID` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '수정자 아이디';
ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_hist MODIFY COLUMN `HIST_USER_NM` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '수정자 이름';
ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_hist MODIFY COLUMN `HIST_USER_IP` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '수정자 아이피';
ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_hist MODIFY COLUMN `HIST_DATE` datetime DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '수정일';
ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_hist MODIFY COLUMN `HIST_TY` char(1) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '수정타입';


--  Table [TAP_AU_AUTHOR_MANAGE]

CREATE TABLE TAP_AU_AUTHOR_MANAGE
(
	SYS_ID           VARCHAR (128) NOT NULL,
	AUTHOR_CODE      INT (16) NOT NULL,
	AUTHOR_NM        VARCHAR (128),
	AUTHOR_SEQ       INT (10) NOT NULL
)
;

ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_manage COMMENT='권한 관리';
ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_manage MODIFY COLUMN `SYS_ID` varchar(128) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '시스템 아이디';
ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_manage MODIFY COLUMN `AUTHOR_CODE` int(16) NOT NULL COMMENT '권한 코드';
ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_manage MODIFY COLUMN `AUTHOR_NM` varchar(128) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci DEFAULT NULL NULL COMMENT '권한명';
ALTER TABLE tap_au_author_manage MODIFY COLUMN `AUTHOR_SEQ` int(10) NOT NULL COMMENT '권한번호';



--  Table [TAP_AU_AUTHOR_MBER] 

CREATE TABLE TAP_AU_AUTHOR_MBER 
(
	AUTHOR_MBER_SEQ  INT (10) NOT NULL,
	MBER_ID          VARCHAR (256) NOT NULL,
	AUTHOR_CODE      INT (16),
	SYS_ID           VARCHAR (128)
)

(

	COLUMN_NM_NO     VARCHAR (200) DEFAULT '번호' NOT NULL,

	COLUMN_NM_REG_NM VARCHAR (200) DEFAULT '작성자' NOT NULL,
	COLUMN_NM_REG_DT VARCHAR (200) DEFAULT '작성일' NOT NULL,
	SECRET_USE_AT    CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'Y' NOT NULL,
	FILE_MXM_CO      INT (3) DEFAULT 10 NOT NULL,
	EDITR_USE_AT     CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'Y' NOT NULL,
	STTUS_USE_AT     CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	NEW_NTT_NTCN_HOUR INT (2) DEFAULT 24 NOT NULL,
	SEARCH_PAGE      INT (10) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,

	STSFDG_USE_AT    CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	INDVDLINFO_COLCT_AGRE_USE_AT CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	INDVDLINFO_COLCT_AGRE_CN VARCHAR (2000) DEFAULT 'N',

	INFO_PROVD_AGRE_CN VARCHAR (2000) DEFAULT 'N',
	FLTER_USE_AT     CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,

	OWNER_LIST_USE_AT CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	NTT_CN_ESSNTL_AT CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	NOTICE_AT        CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	REG_ID           VARCHAR (256) NOT NULL,
	REG_NM           VARCHAR (256) NOT NULL,
	REG_IP           VARCHAR (256) NOT NULL,
	REG_DT           DATETIME,
	BBS_USE_AT       CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'Y' NOT NULL,
	REPLY_AT         CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N',
	CVPL_AT          CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N',
	PRFACE_USE_AT    CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N',

	REGIST_END_DE    DATETIME,

	HIST_GROUP_SEQ   INT (10) NOT NULL,
	HIST_USER_ID     VARCHAR (256) NOT NULL,

--  Table [TAP_BM_BBS_MANAGE] 

CREATE TABLE TAP_BM_BBS_MANAGE 
(
	BBS_ID           INT (10) NOT NULL,
	SYS_ID           VARCHAR (20) NOT NULL,
	BBS_TY           VARCHAR (20) NOT NULL,
	BBS_PRPOS        VARCHAR (20) NOT NULL,
	BBS_SJ           VARCHAR (256) NOT NULL,
	BBS_DC           VARCHAR (2000),
	ANSWER_TY        CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	MENU_COURS       VARCHAR (2000),
	MENU_ID          INT (10),
	PAGE_NTT_CO      INT (3) DEFAULT 10 NOT NULL,
	COLUMN_NM_NO     VARCHAR (200) DEFAULT '번호' NOT NULL,
	COLUMN_NM_CO     VARCHAR (200) DEFAULT '조회수' NOT NULL,
	COLUMN_NM_REG_NM VARCHAR (200) DEFAULT '작성자' NOT NULL,
	COLUMN_NM_REG_DT VARCHAR (200) DEFAULT '작성일' NOT NULL,
	SECRET_USE_AT    CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'Y' NOT NULL,
	FILE_MXM_CO      INT (3) DEFAULT 10 NOT NULL,
	EDITR_USE_AT     CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'Y' NOT NULL,
	STTUS_USE_AT     CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	NEW_NTT_NTCN_HOUR INT (2) DEFAULT 24 NOT NULL,
	SEARCH_PAGE      INT (10) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
	LIST_FILE_DWLD_AT CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	FILE_LMTT_SIZE   INT (5) DEFAULT 20 NOT NULL,
	CONFM_USE_AT     CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	STSFDG_USE_AT    CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	INDVDLINFO_COLCT_AGRE_USE_AT CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	INDVDLINFO_COLCT_AGRE_CN VARCHAR (2000) DEFAULT 'N',
	INFO_PROVD_AGRE_USE_AT CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	INFO_PROVD_AGRE_CN VARCHAR (2000) DEFAULT 'N',
	FLTER_USE_AT     CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	SMS_USE_AT       CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	EMAIL_USE_AT     CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	OWNER_LIST_USE_AT CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	NTT_CN_ESSNTL_AT CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	NOTICE_AT        CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	REG_ID           VARCHAR (256) NOT NULL,
	REG_NM           VARCHAR (256) NOT NULL,
	REG_IP           VARCHAR (256) NOT NULL,
	REG_DT           DATETIME,
	BBS_USE_AT       CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'Y' NOT NULL,
	REPLY_AT         CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N',
	CVPL_AT          CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N',
	PRFACE_USE_AT    CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N',
	PRFACE_CN        VARCHAR (2000),
	ANNYMTY_USE_AT   CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N',
	CLSDR_USE_AT     CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N',
	ATCHMNFL_EXTSN   VARCHAR (2000),
	IPIN_PAGE        VARCHAR (32),
	REGIST_PD_USE_AT CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N',
	REGIST_BEGIN_DE  DATETIME,
	REGIST_END_DE    DATETIME
)
;

--  Table [TCO_NA_NTT_HIST]

(
	BBS_ID           INT (10) NOT NULL,

	UPPER_NTT_SN     INT (10),
	NTT_SJ           VARCHAR (2000),
	NTT_CN           LONGTEXT,

	NTT_USE_AT       CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'Y' NOT NULL,
	SECRET_AT        CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	SMS_AT           CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	EMAIL_AT         CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	NOTICE_AT        CHAR (1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	NOTICE_BEGIN_DT  DATETIME,
	NOTICE_END_DT    DATETIME,
	ADIT_COL1        VARCHAR (512),
	ADIT_COL2        VARCHAR (512),
	ADIT_COL3        VARCHAR (512),
	ADIT_COL4        VARCHAR (512),
	ADIT_COL5        VARCHAR (512),
	ADIT_COL6        VARCHAR (512),
	ADIT_COL7        VARCHAR (512),
	ADIT_COL8        VARCHAR (512),
	ADIT_COL9        VARCHAR (512),
	ADIT_COL10       VARCHAR (512),
	CLSDR_AT         CHAR (1),
	BEFORE_ID        INT (10),
	CONFM_AT         CHAR (1),
	CONFM_BEGIN_DT   DATETIME,

	UPDT_DT		DATETIME NULL COMMENT '최종 수정일',

);
